```dafny
// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||

  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');

      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

Now for a<=b case:

- assert 2 * b >= val; Wait val = max(2*a,b). Since a <= b, 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b? Actually 2*b >= b. So 2*b >= max(2*a,b). So it's true.

- assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s'); We need to show that this conjunction cannot hold. Since s' < val = max(2*a,b). We consider two subcases: If val = 2*a (when 2*a >= b), then s' < 2*a, so 2*a <= s' is false. So conjunction false. If val = b (when b > 2*a), then s' < b, so b <= s' false. So in any case, conjunction false. So the assert holds.

- assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s'); Since s' < max(2*a,b). If val = 2*a, then s' < 2*a, but a <= s'? Could hold? Let's analyze. In this case val=2*a, and b <= 2*a? Not necessarily. But we need to show that the conjunction fails. Let's consider subcases.

Case1: val=2*a. That means 2*a >= b. So b <= 2*a. But s' < 2*a, so s' < 2*a. We need to see if 2*b <= s' could hold. Since b <= 2*a, 2*b <= 4*a. But s' < 2*a, so 2*b <= s' implies 2*b < 2*a, so b < a. But a <= b, so impossible. So 2*b <= s' cannot hold. So conjunction false.

Case2: val=b. That means b > 2*a. Then s' < b. For a <= s' to hold, s' >= a. But s' < b. So a <= s' < b. Then 2*b <= s' cannot hold because 2*b > b > s'. So conjunction false. So assertion holds.

- assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s'); This is symmetrical to previous but with 2*b and a. Since s' < max(2*a,b). If val=2*a: s' < 2*a. 2*b <= s'? Since b <= 2*a (since val=2*a >= b). So 2*b <= 2*a? That would mean 2*b <= s' < 2*a. For 2*b <= s', need 2*b < 2*a => b < a, impossible. So false. If val=b: s' < b. 2*b <= s' impossible. So false.

- assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s'); This is same as disjunct 1: need to show max(2*a,b) > s'. Since val = max(2*a,b) > s' holds by s' < val. So assertion holds.

Now else case a > b:

- assert 2 * a >= val; val = max(2*b,a). Since a > b, 2*a >= 2*b, and a <= 2*a, but val <= 2*a? Let's check: val = max(2*b,a). Since a > b, 2*b < 2*a, but maybe a > 2*b? Not necessarily. But val <= max(2*a,a) = 2*a. So val <= 2*a. So 2*a >= val holds.

- assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s'); Since s' < val <= 2*a, s' < 2*a, so 2*a <= s' false. So conjunction false.

- assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s'); Since s' < val <= 2*a. But if val = a (when a >= 2*b), s' < a, so a <= s' false. If val = 2*b (when 2*b > a), s' < 2*b, so 2*b <= s' false. So false.

- assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s'); Similar reasoning.

- assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s'); Since s' < val <= 2*a, 2*a <= s' false. So false.

Thus all assertions hold.

However, there might be a problem: In the forall, we used "forall s' | 1 <= s' < val ensures !CanFitInSquare(a,b,s')". The "ensures" clause is inside the forall body? The syntax is:

forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val ensures !CanFitInSquare(a,b,s') { ... }

But in Dafny, the syntax is:

forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val :: !CanFitInSquare(a,b,s') { ... }

Or we can use "forall s' | 1 <= s' < val :: !CanFitInSquare(a,b,s')" with no body? Wait in Dafny, "forall ... ensures" inside a method is used for quantifiers in pre/post-conditions? Actually inside a method body, we can write:

forall x :: P(x) { ... } // This is a quantifier that expects a body for a proof obligation.

But the syntax "forall x | P(x) ensures Q(x)" is for quantifiers in a specification (pre/post). But inside a method body, we can just use:

forall s' :: 1 <=

// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)

  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b

  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {

    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;

  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

      assert 2 * b >= val;

      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');

      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are

```dafny
// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{

  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||

  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(s' >= a + b); // s' < val <= a+b
    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');

      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');

      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);

    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works

    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

      assert 2 * a <= val || b <= val; // derived from val definition

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' :: 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')

<DAFNY_CODE>
```dafny
// Two rectangles placed side by side (separated along x-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total width = w1 + w2; each height must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

// Two rectangles stacked (separated along y-axis) in a square of side s.
// Total height = h1 + h2; each width must fit within s.
ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

// Whether two identical a×b rectangles (axis-parallel, possibly rotated) can be
// placed inside a square of side s without overlapping.
// By the separating axis theorem, non-overlapping axis-aligned rectangles are
// separated along at least one axis. We enumerate all orientation pairs
// {(a,b),(b,a)}^2 and both separation directions.
ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

// s is the smallest square side length that can contain two a×b rectangles
ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val; // because val >= 2*a
    assert b <= val;     // because val >= b
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val; // because val >= 2*b
    assert a <= val;     // because val >= a
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
```

  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // If a + b <= s', then the rectangle would fit by side-by-side or stacked.
    // Since s' < val <= a + b, we have !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s').
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
      // Since s' < val, either 2*a > s' or b > s'.
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // For the mixed orientation case (b,a):
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // For stacked configurations:
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;

      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');

      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;

      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;

ghost predicate FitsSideBySide(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 + w2 <= s && h1 <= s && h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate FitsStacked(w1: int, h1: int, w2: int, h2: int, s: int)
{
  w1 <= s && w2 <= s && h1 + h2 <= s
}

ghost predicate CanFitInSquare(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(b, a, b, a, s)
}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  // Because 2*lo = 2*min(a,b) <= min(a,b) + max(a,b) = a+b
  // and hi = max(a,b) <= a+b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

  FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, a, b, s) ||
  FitsSideBySide(a, b, b, a, s) || FitsStacked(a, b, b, a, s) ||

}

ghost predicate IsMinimalSide(a: int, b: int, s: int)
{
  CanFitInSquare(a, b, s) && forall s' :: 1 <= s' < s ==> !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');

      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }

  area := val * val;

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  if a <= b {
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  assert val <= a + b;

  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');

      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}

method MinimalSquare(a: int, b: int) returns (area: int)
  requires 1 <= a && 1 <= b
  ensures exists s :: 1 <= s && area == s * s && IsMinimalSide(a, b, s)
{
  var lo := if a < b then a else b;
  var hi := if a < b then b else a;
  var val := if 2 * lo > hi then 2 * lo else hi;

  // val = max(2*lo, hi) where lo = min(a,b), hi = max(a,b)
  assert val >= 1;
  assert lo <= hi;

  // Show CanFitInSquare(a, b, val)
  if a <= b {
    // lo == a, hi == b, val == max(2*a, b)
    assert 2 * a <= val && b <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(a, b, a, b, val);
  } else {
    // lo == b, hi == a, val == max(2*b, a)
    assert 2 * b <= val && a <= val;
    assert FitsSideBySide(b, a, b, a, val);
  }
  assert CanFitInSquare(a, b, val);

  // Key inequality: val <= a + b
  assert val <= a + b;

  // Show minimality: no smaller square works
  forall s' | 1 <= s' < val
    ensures !CanFitInSquare(a, b, s')
  {
    // s' < val <= a+b, so mixed-orientation configs fail
    assert !(a + b <= s');

    if a <= b {
      // val = max(2*a, b). Since a <= b: 2*b >= 2*a and 2*b >= b, so 2*b >= val
      assert 2 * b >= val;
      // Disjunct 1: FitsSideBySide(a,b,a,b,s') needs 2*a <= s' && b <= s'
      // s' < max(2*a, b) means !(2*a <= s' && b <= s')
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      // Disjunct 2: FitsStacked(a,b,a,b,s') needs a <= s' && 2*b <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      // Disjunct 7: FitsSideBySide(b,a,b,a,s') needs 2*b <= s' && a <= s'
      // s' < 2*b, so fails
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      // Disjunct 8: FitsStacked(b,a,b,a,s') needs b <= s' && 2*a <= s'
      // Same as disjunct 1 requirement: max(2*a, b) > s'
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    } else {
      // val = max(2*b, a). Since a > b: 2*a > 2*b and 2*a >= a, so 2*a >= val
      assert 2 * a >= val;
      assert !(2 * a <= s' && b <= s');
      assert !(a <= s' && 2 * b <= s');
      assert !(2 * b <= s' && a <= s');
      assert !(b <= s' && 2 * a <= s');
    }
  }

  area := val * val;
}
